         .               /// Fast path helper for testing if a type is `Sized`.
         .               ///

         .               ///
         .               /// Note that we could never rely on the fact that a type such as `[_]` is

         .               /// can be called, but that doesn't mean it shouldn't typecheck. This is why

         .                       | ty::RawPtr(..)
-- line 2246 ----------------------------------------
-- line 2250 ----------------------------------------
         .                       | ty::GeneratorWitness(..)
